different_country_flags_category = {


	##USA
	USA_western_conservatism_flag = {

		icon = GFX_decision_generic_form_nation
		
		cost = 10
		
		ai_will_do = {
			factor = 1
		}

		allowed = {
			original_tag = USA
		}
		visible = {
			original_tag = USA
			has_country_leader_with_trait = western_conservatism
			NOT = {
				has_cosmetic_tag = USA_western_flag
			}
		}

		complete_effect = {
			log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: Decision USA_western_conservatism_flag"
			set_cosmetic_tag = USA_western_flag
			custom_effect_tooltip = tooltip_change_flag
		}
	}
